Task instruction sent to agent 
# Task: Extract Shared Foreach Optimizer Step

## Objective
Extract the repeated `_multi_tensor_*` foreach optimization patterns from individual
optimizer files (sgd.py, adam.py, adamw.py, etc.) into a shared
`torch/optim/_foreach.py` module.

## Requirements

1. **Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py`**:
   - `_foreach_optimizer_step(params, grads, step_fn, **kwargs)` function
   - Common foreach/fused parameter handling logic
   - Shared gradient scaling and clipping utilities

2. **Update optimizer files** to use the shared module:
   - `torch/optim/sgd.py`
   - `torch/optim/adam.py`
   - `torch/optim/adamw.py`
   - Others that have `_multi_tensor_` functions

3. **Keep backward compatibility**: existing public APIs unchanged

## Key Reference Files
- `torch/optim/sgd.py` — `_multi_tensor_sgd` function
- `torch/optim/adam.py` — `_multi_tensor_adam` function
- `torch/optim/adamw.py` — `_multi_tensor_adamw` function
- `torch/optim/_functional.py` — functional optimizer implementations

## Success Criteria
- `torch/optim/_foreach.py` exists with shared logic
- At least 3 optimizer files import from _foreach
- Duplicate foreach patterns reduced
- Original optimizer APIs still work

def _multi_tensor_rmsprop(
    params: list[Tensor],
    grads: list[Tensor],
    square_avgs: list[Tensor],
    grad_avgs: list[Tensor],
    momentum_buffer_list: list[Tensor],
    state_steps: list[Tensor],
    *,
    lr: float,
    alpha: float,
    eps: float,
    weight_decay: float,
    momentum: float,
    centered: bool,
    maximize: bool,
    differentiable: bool,
    capturable: bool,
    has_complex: bool,
):
    if len(params) == 0:
        return

    assert not differentiable, "_foreach ops don't support autograd"

    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]
    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:
        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()
        assert all(
            p.device.type == step.device.type
            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices
            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)
        ), (
            f"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}."
        )

    lr = _to_scalar(lr)

    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(
        [params, grads, square_avgs, grad_avgs, momentum_buffer_list, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]
    )
    for (
        (
            grouped_params_,
            grouped_grads_,
            grouped_square_avgs_,
            grouped_grad_avgs_,
            grouped_momentum_buffer_list_,
            grouped_state_steps_,
        )
    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():
        grouped_params = cast(list[Tensor], grouped_params_)

def _multi_tensor_sgd(
    params: list[Tensor],
    grads: list[Tensor],
    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],
    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],
    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],
    *,
    weight_decay: float,
    momentum: float,
    lr: float,
    dampening: float,
    nesterov: bool,
    maximize: bool,
    has_sparse_grad: bool,
):
    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None

    if len(params) == 0:
        return

    lr = _to_scalar(lr)

    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(
        [params, grads, momentum_buffer_list],  # type: ignore[list-item]
        with_indices=True,
    )
    for (
        device_params_,
        device_grads_,
        device_momentum_buffer_list,
    ), indices in grouped_tensors.values():
        device_params: list[Tensor] = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)
        device_grads: list[Tensor] = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)

        device_has_sparse_grad = has_sparse_grad and any(
            grad.is_sparse for grad in device_grads
        )

        if maximize:
            device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]

        if weight_decay != 0:

                    device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay

   473→def _fused_sgd(
   474→    params: list[Tensor],
   475→    grads: list[Tensor],
   476→    momentum_buffer_list: list[Optional[Tensor]],
   477→    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],
   478→    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],
   479→    *,
   480→    weight_decay: float,
   481→    momentum: float,
   482→    lr: float,
   483→    dampening: float,
   484→    nesterov: bool,
   485→    maximize: bool,
   486→    has_sparse_grad: bool,
   487→) -> None:
   488→    if not params:
   489→        return
   490→    if has_sparse_grad:
   491→        raise RuntimeError("`_fused_sgd` does not support sparse gradients")
   492→    grad_scale_dict: DeviceDict = (
   493→        {grad_scale.device: grad_scale} if grad_scale is not None else {}
   494→    )
   495→    found_inf_dict: DeviceDict = (
   496→        {found_inf.device: found_inf} if found_inf is not None else {}
   497→    )
   498→
   499→    no_momentum_buffer = momentum == 0
   500→    is_first_step = (
   501→        all(t is None for t in momentum_buffer_list) and not no_momentum_buffer
   502→    )
   503→    if is_first_step:
   504→        for i, g in enumerate(grads):
   505→            momentum_buffer_list[i] = torch.empty_like(g)
   506→    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(
   507→        [params, grads, momentum_buffer_list],  # type: ignore[list-item]
   508→        with_indices=False,
   509→    )
   510→    for (device, _), (
   511→        (device_params_, device_grads_, device_momentum_buffer_list),
   512→        _,
   513→    ) in grouped_tensors.items():
   514→        device_params: list[Tensor] = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)
   515→        device_grads: list[Tensor] = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)
   516→        device_grad_scale, device_found_inf = None, N

## Summary: PyTorch Optimizer Module Utilities for Reuse in _foreach.py

I've completed a thorough examination of the PyTorch optimizer module. Here's a comprehensive list of utilities organized by category that could be reused in a shared `_foreach.py` module:

## **1. DEVICE AND DTYPE GROUPING UTILITIES**

### **`_group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype`**
- **Location**: `/workspace/torch/optim/optimizer.py` (lines 531-545), imported from `torch.utils._foreach_utils`
- **Signature**:
  ```python
  def _group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(
      tensorlistlist: TensorListList,
      with_indices: bool = False,
  ) -> Union[
      dict[tuple[None, None], tuple[TensorListList, Indices]],
      dict[tuple[torch.device, torch.dtype], tuple[TensorListList, Indices]],
  ]
  ```
- **Purpose**: Groups a list of lists of tensors by device and dtype. Skips grouping during torch.compile and returns a single group with indices.
- **Used By**: All modern optimizers (Adam, SGD, Adagrad, RMSprop, etc.)
- **Key Feature**: When compiling, returns `{(None, None): (tensorlistlist, indices)}` for torch.compile optimization
- **Type Aliases Required**: `TensorListList`, `Indices` (from `torch.utils._foreach_utils`)

### **`DeviceDict`** (Type Alias)
- **Definition**: `dict[Optional[torch.device], torch.Tensor]`
- **Purpose**: Mapping from device to tensors (used for hyperparameter tensors like lr, beta1, etc.)
- **Used By**: Adam, _multi_tensor implementations for handling tensor hyperparameters

### **`DeviceDtypeDict`** (Type Alias)
- **Definition**: `dict[Optional[tuple[torch.device, torch.dtype]], torch.Tensor]`
- **Purpose**: Mapping from (device, dtype) tuple to tensors
- **Used By**: Single tensor implem

          add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise RuntimeError(\n                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if lr.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n\n    # Hinton.\n   237\u2192    and centered version `Generating Sequences\n   238\u2192    With Recurrent Neural Networks <https://arxiv.org/pdf/1308.0850v5.pdf>`_.\n   239\u2192    The implementation here takes the square root of the gradient average before\n   240\u2192    adding epsilon (note that TensorFlow interchanges these two operations). The effective\n   241\u2192    learning rate is thus :math:`\\gamma/(\\sqrt{v} + \\epsilon)` where :math:`\\gamma`\n   242\u2192    is the scheduled learning rate and :math:`v` is the weighted moving Input
{
  "content": "# Task: Extract Shared Foreach Optimizer Step\n\n## Context\nThe PyTorch optimizer implementations contain repeated `_multi_tensor_*` patterns across 11+ optimizer files. These functions have common preprocessing patterns that can be extracted to reduce duplication.\n\n## Exploration Results\n\n### Common Patterns Found Across _multi_tensor_* Functions\n1. **Empty parameter check**: All return early if `len(params) == 0`\n2. **LR scalar conversion**: `lr = _to_scalar(lr)`\n3. **Tensor grouping**: `Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype([...], with_indices=True)`\n4. **Maximize handling**: `if maximize: device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)`\n5. **Weight decay**: Memory-optimized addition with reuse of intermediate tensors\n6. **Assertions**: `assert not differentiable` and `assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None`\n7. **Complex dtype handling**: `_view_as_real(...)` pattern\n8. **CPU step optimization**: Avoid repeated tensor wrapping for CPU-resident state\n\n### Utilities Available for Reuse\nFrom `torch.optim.optimizer`:\n- `_to_scalar()` - Convert tensor LR to scalar\n- `_get_value()` - Extract Python value from tensor\n- `_view_as_real()` - Convert complex tensors for processing\n- `_get_scalar_dtype()`, `_get_capturable_supported_devices()`\n- Type aliases: `DeviceDict`, `DeviceDtypeDict`\n- `Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype()` - Core grouping utility\n\n### Optimizer-Specific Differences\n- **SGD**: Momentum buffer handling, sparse gradient fallback\n- **Adam**: Parameter validation, step increment, decoupled weight decay, AMSGrad logic\n- **RMSprop**: Complex handling, centered variance, CPU step optimization\n- **Adagrad**: Sparse gradient fallback, LR decay per parameter\n- Each has distinct bias correction and state update logic that can't be fully abstracted\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Approach: Helper Functions + Callback-based Framework\n\nCreate `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` with:\n\n1. **Helper functions for common operations**:\n   - `_foreach_apply_maximize(device_grads, maximize)` - Negate gradients if maximizing\n   - `_foreach_apply_weight_decay(device_grads, device_params, weight_decay, maximize)` - Memory-optimized weight decay\n   - `_foreach_group_tensors_and_prepare(params, grads, state_tensors, maximize, weight_decay, **kwargs)` - Groups and preprocesses tensors\n\n2. **Main callback-based orchestration function**:\n   - `_foreach_optimizer_step(params, grads, step_fn, state_tensors, **kwargs)`\n   - Handles grouping, assertions, maximize, weight decay\n   - Calls `step_fn(device_params, device_grads, device_states, indices, **kwargs)` for optimizer-specific logic\n\n3. **Common utility functions**:\n   - `_get_group_device_dtype()` - Extract device/dtype from grouped tensors\n   - `_validate_foreach_hyperparams()` - Common validation for tensor hyperparameters\n\n### Files to Modify\n\n**Primary**:\n- Create: `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` with shared logic\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/sgd.py` - Use _foreach_optimizer_step\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adam.py` - Use _foreach_optimizer_step\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adamw.py` - Inherits from Adam (automatic)\n\n**Secondary** (to meet \u22653 file requirement + reduce duplication):\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adagrad.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/rmsprop.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/radam.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adadelta.py` - Use shared helpers\n\n## Detailed Implementation Plan\n\n### Step 1: Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py`\n\n```python\n# torch/optim/_foreach.py\nfrom typing import Callable, cast, Optional, Union, Any\nimport torch\nfrom torch import Tensor\nfrom .optimizer import (\n    _to_scalar, _get_value, _view_as_real,\n    Optimizer, DeviceDict, DeviceDtypeDict\n)\n\n# Helper functions\ndef _foreach_apply_maximize(\n    device_grads: list[Tensor],\n    maximize: bool\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Apply maximize (negate grads) and return modified grads.\"\"\"\n    if maximize:\n        return torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n    return device_grads\n\ndef _foreach_apply_weight_decay(\n    device_grads: list[Tensor],\n    device_params: list[Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    can_reuse_grads: bool = True\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Apply weight decay to gradients with memory optimization.\n\n    When maximize has already allocated new memory for device_grads,\n    we can reuse that memory. Otherwise, allocate new memory.\n    \"\"\"\n    if weight_decay == 0:\n        return device_grads\n\n    # Reuse device_grads memory if it was already allocated for maximize\n    if can_reuse_grads and maximize:\n        torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        return device_grads\n    else:\n        return torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n            device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n        )\n\ndef _foreach_optimizer_step(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    step_fn: Callable[..., None],\n    state_tensors: dict[str, list[Optional[Tensor]]],\n    has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n    maximize: bool = False,\n    weight_decay: float = 0.0,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor] = 1e-3,\n    **kwargs: Any\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    Shared foreach optimizer step with common preprocessing.\n\n    Args:\n        params: List of parameters to optimize\n        grads: List of gradients\n        step_fn: Callback function that implements optimizer-specific logic\n        state_tensors: Dict mapping state names to lists of state tensors\n        has_sparse_grad: Whether sparse gradients are possible\n        maximize: Whether to maximize loss instead of minimize\n        weight_decay: Weight decay factor\n        lr: Learning rate\n        **kwargs: Additional arguments passed to step_fn\n    \"\"\"\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n\n    # Group all tensors by device and dtype\n    tensors_to_group = [params, grads] + list(state_tensors.values())\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        tensors_to_group,\n        with_indices=True,\n    )\n\n    for grouped_tensors_tuple, indices in grouped_tensors.values():\n        # Extract grouped tensors\n        device_params_ = grouped_tensors_tuple[0]\n        device_grads_ = grouped_tensors_tuple[1]\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n\n        # Extract state tensors\n        device_states = {}\n        for i, (state_name, state_list) in enumerate(state_tensors.items(), start=2):\n            device_states[state_name] = cast(list[Optional[Tensor]], grouped_tensors_tuple[i])\n\n        # Check for sparse gradients in this device group\n        device_has_sparse_grad = has_sparse_grad and any(\n            grad.is_sparse for grad in device_grads\n        )\n\n        # Apply maximize\n        device_grads = _foreach_apply_maximize(device_grads, maximize)\n\n        # Apply weight decay\n        device_grads = _foreach_apply_weight_decay(\n            device_grads, device_params, weight_decay, maximize\n        )\n\n        # Call optimizer-specific step function\n        step_fn(\n            device_params=device_params,\n            device_grads=device_grads,\n            device_states=device_states,\n            device_has_sparse_grad=device_has_sparse_grad,\n            indices=indices,\n            lr=lr,\n            **kwargs\n        )\n```\n\n### Step 2: Refactor SGD's `_multi_tensor_sgd`\n\nReplace the common preprocessing with `_foreach_optimizer_step` while keeping momentum-specific logic.\n\n### Step 3: Refactor Adam's `_multi_tensor_adam`\n\nApply same pattern, keeping Adam-specific logic (step increment, bias correction, AMSGrad).\n\n### Step 4: Update Other Optimizers\n\nIncrementally refactor Adagrad, RMSprop, RAdam to use shared helpers.\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **Callback approach**: Keep optimizer-specific logic in a step_fn callback to avoid forcing all optimizers into the same mold\n2. **Memory efficiency**: Maintain the existing memory-reuse optimization (e.g., reusing device_grads when maximize is applied)\n3. **Gradual refactoring**: Don't require all optimizers to change at once; allow phased migration\n4. **Backward compatibility**: Existing public APIs unchanged; only internal _multi_tensor_* functions refactored\n5. **Type safety**: Use cast() appropriately and preserve existing type hints\n\n## Testing Strategy\n\n1. Run existing optimizer tests: `python -m pytest test/test_optim.py -xvs`\n2. Verify numerical equivalence between old and new implementations\n3. Check that state_dict serialization still works\n4. Ensure hook APIs still fire in correct order\n5. The _foreach_optimizer_step function signature is flexible to accept any state tensors\n2. Each optimizer's step_fn is responsible for its own logic (momentum, exponential moving averages, etc.)\n3.   "content": "# Task: Extract Shared Foreach Optimizer Step\n\n## Context\nThe PyTorch optimizer implementations contain repeated `_multi_tensor_*` patterns across 11+ optimizer files. These functions have common preprocessing patterns that can be extracted to reduce duplication.\n\n## Exploration Results\n\n### Common Patterns Found Across _multi_tensor_* Functions\n1. **Empty parameter check**: All return early if `len(params) == 0`\n2. **LR scalar conversion**: `lr = _to_scalar(lr)`\n3. **Tensor grouping**: `Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype([...], with_indices=True)`\n4. **Maximize handling**: `if maximize: device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)`\n5. **Weight decay**: Memory-optimized addition with reuse of intermediate tensors\n6. **Assertions**: `assert not differentiable` and `assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None`\n7. **Complex dtype handling**: `_view_as_real(...)` pattern\n8. **CPU step optimization**: Avoid repeated tensor wrapping for CPU-resident state\n\n### Utilities Available for Reuse\nFrom `torch.optim.optimizer`:\n- `_to_scalar()` - Convert tensor LR to scalar\n- `_get_value()` - Extract Python value from tensor\n- `_view_as_real()` - Convert complex tensors for processing\n- `_get_scalar_dtype()`, `_get_capturable_supported_devices()`\n- Type aliases: `DeviceDict`, `DeviceDtypeDict`\n- `Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype()` - Core grouping utility\n\n### Optimizer-Specific Differences\n- **SGD**: Momentum buffer handling, sparse gradient fallback\n- **Adam**: Parameter validation, step increment, decoupled weight decay, AMSGrad logic\n- **RMSprop**: Complex handling, centered variance, CPU step optimization\n- **Adagrad**: Sparse gradient fallback, LR decay per parameter\n- Each has distinct bias correction and state update logic that can't be fully abstracted\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Approach: Helper Functions + Callback-based Framework\n\nCreate `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` with:\n\n1. **Helper functions for common operations**:\n   - `_foreach_apply_maximize(device_grads, maximize)` - Negate gradients if maximizing\n   - `_foreach_apply_weight_decay(device_grads, device_params, weight_decay, maximize)` - Memory-optimized weight decay\n   - `_foreach_group_tensors_and_prepare(params, grads, state_tensors, maximize, weight_decay, **kwargs)` - Groups and preprocesses tensors\n\n2. **Main callback-based orchestration function**:\n   - `_foreach_optimizer_step(params, grads, step_fn, state_tensors, **kwargs)`\n   - Handles grouping, assertions, maximize, weight decay\n   - Calls `step_fn(device_params, device_grads, device_states, indices, **kwargs)` for optimizer-specific logic\n\n3. **Common utility functions**:\n   - `_get_group_device_dtype()` - Extract device/dtype from grouped tensors\n   - `_validate_foreach_hyperparams()` - Common validation for tensor hyperparameters\n\n### Files to Modify\n\n**Primary**:\n- Create: `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` with shared logic\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/sgd.py` - Use _foreach_optimizer_step\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adam.py` - Use _foreach_optimizer_step\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adamw.py` - Inherits from Adam (automatic)\n\n**Secondary** (to meet \u22653 file requirement + reduce duplication):\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adagrad.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/rmsprop.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/radam.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adadelta.py` - Use shared helpers\n\n## Detailed Implementation Plan\n\n### Step 1: Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py`\n\n```python\n# torch/optim/_foreach.py\nfrom typing import Callable, cast, Optional, Union, Any\nimport torch\nfrom torch import Tensor\nfrom .optimizer import (\n    _to_scalar, _get_value, _view_as_real,\n    Optimizer, DeviceDict, DeviceDtypeDict\n)\n\n# Helper functions\ndef _foreach_apply_maximize(\n    device_grads: list[Tensor],\n    maximize: bool\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Apply maximize (negate grads) and return modified grads.\"\"\"\n    if maximize:\n        return torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n    return device_grads\n\ndef _foreach_apply_weight_decay(\n    device_grads: list[Tensor],\n    device_params: list[Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    can_reuse_grads: bool = True\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Apply weight decay to gradients with memory optimization.\n\n    When maximize has already allocated new memory for device_grads,\n    we can reuse that memory. Otherwise, allocate new memory.\n    \"\"\"\n    if weight_decay == 0:\n        return device_grads\n\n    # Reuse device_grads memory if it was already allocated for maximize\n    if can_reuse_grads and maximize:\n        torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        return device_grads\n    else:\n        return torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n            device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n        )\n\ndef _foreach_optimizer_step(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    step_fn: Callable[..., None],\n    state_tensors: dict[str, list[Optional[Tensor]]],\n    has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n    maximize: bool = False,\n    weight_decay: float = 0.0,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor] = 1e-3,\n    **kwargs: Any\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    Shared foreach optimizer step with common preprocessing.\n\n    Args:\n        params: List of parameters to optimize\n        grads: List of gradients\n        step_fn: Callback function that implements optimizer-specific logic\n        state_tensors: Dict mapping state names to lists of state tensors\n        has_sparse_grad: Whether sparse gradients are possible\n        maximize: Whether to maximize loss instead of minimize\n        weight_decay: Weight decay factor\n        lr: Learning rate\n        **kwargs: Additional arguments passed to step_fn\n    \"\"\"\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n\n    # Group all tensors by device and dtype\n    tensors_to_group = [params, grads] + list(state_tensors.values())\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        tensors_to_group,\n        with_indices=True,\n    )\n\n    for grouped_tensors_tuple, indices in grouped_tensors.values():\n        # Extract grouped tensors\n        device_params_ = grouped_tensors_tuple[0]\n        device_grads_ = grouped_tensors_tuple[1]\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n\n        # Extract state tensors\n        device_states = {}\n        for i, (state_name, state_list) in enumerate(state_tensors.items(), start=2):\n            device_states[state_name] = cast(list[Optional[Tensor]], grouped_tensors_tuple[i])\n\n        # Check for sparse gradients in this device group\n        device_has_sparse_grad = has_sparse_grad and any(\n            grad.is_sparse for grad in device_grads\n        )\n\n        # Apply maximize\n        device_grads = _foreach_apply_maximize(device_grads, maximize)\n\n        # Apply weight decay\n        device_grads = _foreach_apply_weight_decay(\n            device_grads, device_params, weight_decay, maximize\n        )\n\n        # Call optimizer-specific step function\n        step_fn(\n            device_params=device_params,\n            device_grads=device_grads,\n            device_states=device_states,\n            device_has_sparse_grad=device_has_sparse_grad,\n            indices=indices,\n            lr=lr,\n            **kwargs\n        )\n```\n\n### Step 2: Refactor SGD's `_multi_tensor_sgd`\n\nReplace the common preprocessing with `_foreach_optimizer_step` while keeping momentum-specific logic.\n\n### Step 3: Refactor Adam's `_multi_tensor_adam`\n\nApply same pattern, keeping Adam-specific logic (step increment, bias correction, AMSGrad).\n\n### Step 4: Update Other Optimizers\n\nIncrementally refactor Adagrad, RMSprop, RAdam to use shared helpers.\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **Callback approach**: Keep optimizer-specific logic in a step_fn callback to avoid forcing all optimizers into the same mold\n2. **Memory efficiency**: Maintain the existing memory-reuse optimization (e.g., reusing device_grads when maximize is applied)\n3. **Gradual refactoring**: Don't require all optimizers to change at once; allow phased migration\n4. **Backward compatibility**: Existing public APIs unchanged; only internal _multi_tensor_* functions refactored\n5. **Type safety**: Use cast() appropriately and preserve existing type hints\n\n## Testing Strategy\n\n1. Run existing optimizer tests: `python -m pytest test/test_optim.py -xvs`\n2. Verify numerical equivalence between old and new implementations\n3. Check that state_dict serialization still works\n4. Ensure hook APIs still fire in correct order\n5.         "+    return device_grads",

  "plan": "# Task: Extract Shared Foreach Optimizer Step\n\n## Context\nThe PyTorch optimizer implementations contain repeated `_multi_tensor_*` patterns across 11+ optimizer files. These functions have common preprocessing patterns that can be extracted to reduce duplication.\n\n## Exploration Results\n\n### Common Patterns Found Across _multi_tensor_* Functions\n1. **Empty parameter check**: All return early if `len(params) == 0`\n2. **LR scalar conversion**: `lr = _to_scalar(lr)`\n3. **Tensor grouping**: `Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype([...], with_indices=True)`\n4. **Maximize handling**: `if maximize: device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)`\n5. **Weight decay**: Memory-optimized addition with reuse of intermediate tensors\n6. **Assertions**: `assert not differentiable` and `assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None`\n7. **Complex dtype handling**: `_view_as_real(...)` pattern\n8. **CPU step optimization**: Avoid repeated tensor wrapping for CPU-resident state\n\n### Utilities Available for Reuse\nFrom `torch.optim.optimizer`:\n- `_to_scalar()` - Convert tensor LR to scalar\n- `_get_value()` - Extract Python value from tensor\n- `_view_as_real()` - Convert complex tensors for processing\n- `_get_scalar_dtype()`, `_get_capturable_supported_devices()`\n- Type aliases: `DeviceDict`, `DeviceDtypeDict`\n- `Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype()` - Core grouping utility\n\n### Optimizer-Specific Differences\n- **SGD**: Momentum buffer handling, sparse gradient fallback\n- **Adam**: Parameter validation, step increment, decoupled weight decay, AMSGrad logic\n- **RMSprop**: Complex handling, centered variance, CPU step optimization\n- **Adagrad**: Sparse gradient fallback, LR decay per parameter\n- Each has distinct bias correction and state update logic that can't be fully abstracted\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Approach: Helper Functions + Callback-based Framework\n\nCreate `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` with:\n\n1. **Helper functions for common operations**:\n   - `_foreach_apply_maximize(device_grads, maximize)` - Negate gradients if maximizing\n   - `_foreach_apply_weight_decay(device_grads, device_params, weight_decay, maximize)` - Memory-optimized weight decay\n   - `_foreach_group_tensors_and_prepare(params, grads, state_tensors, maximize, weight_decay, **kwargs)` - Groups and preprocesses tensors\n\n2. **Main callback-based orchestration function**:\n   - `_foreach_optimizer_step(params, grads, step_fn, state_tensors, **kwargs)`\n   - Handles grouping, assertions, maximize, weight decay\n   - Calls `step_fn(device_params, device_grads, device_states, indices, **kwargs)` for optimizer-specific logic\n\n3. **Common utility functions**:\n   - `_get_group_device_dtype()` - Extract device/dtype from grouped tensors\n   - `_validate_foreach_hyperparams()` - Common validation for tensor hyperparameters\n\n### Files to Modify\n\n**Primary**:\n- Create: `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` with shared logic\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/sgd.py` - Use _foreach_optimizer_step\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adam.py` - Use _foreach_optimizer_step\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adamw.py` - Inherits from Adam (automatic)\n\n**Secondary** (to meet \u22653 file requirement + reduce duplication):\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adagrad.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/rmsprop.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/radam.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adadelta.py` - Use shared helpers\n\n## Detailed Implementation Plan\n\n### Step 1: Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py`\n\n```python\n# torch/optim/_foreach.py\nfrom typing import Callable, cast, Optional, Union, Any\nimport torch\nfrom torch import Tensor\nfrom .optimizer import (\n    _to_scalar, _get_value, _view_as_real,\n    Optimizer, DeviceDict, DeviceDtypeDict\n)\n\n# Helper functions\ndef _foreach_apply_maximize(\n    device_grads: list[Tensor],\n    maximize: bool\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Apply maximize (negate grads) and return modified grads.\"\"\"\n    if maximize:\n        return torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n    return device_grads\n\ndef _foreach_apply_weight_decay(\n    device_grads: list[Tensor],\n    device_params: list[Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    can_reuse_grads: bool = True\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Apply weight decay to gradients with memory optimization.\n\n    When maximize has already allocated new memory for device_grads,\n    we can reuse that memory. Otherwise, allocate new memory.\n    \"\"\"\n    if weight_decay == 0:\n        return device_grads\n\n    # Reuse device_grads memory if it was already allocated for maximize\n    if can_reuse_grads and maximize:\n        torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        return device_grads\n    else:\n        return torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n            device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n        )\n\ndef _foreach_optimizer_step(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    step_fn: Callable[..., None],\n    state_tensors: dict[str, list[Optional[Tensor]]],\n    has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n    maximize: bool = False,\n    weight_decay: float = 0.0,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor] = 1e-3,\n    **kwargs: Any\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    Shared foreach optimizer step with common preprocessing.\n\n    Args:\n        params: List of parameters to optimize\n        grads: List of gradients\n        step_fn: Callback function that implements optimizer-specific logic\n        state_tensors: Dict mapping state names to lists of state tensors\n        has_sparse_grad: Whether sparse gradients are possible\n        maximize: Whether to maximize loss instead of minimize\n        weight_decay: Weight decay factor\n        lr: Learning rate\n        **kwargs: Additional arguments passed to step_fn\n    \"\"\"\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n\n    # Group all tensors by device and dtype\n    tensors_to_group = [params, grads] + list(state_tensors.values())\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        tensors_to_group,\n        with_indices=True,\n    )\n\n    for grouped_tensors_tuple, indices in grouped_tensors.values():\n        # Extract grouped tensors\n        device_params_ = grouped_tensors_tuple[0]\n        device_grads_ = grouped_tensors_tuple[1]\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n\n        # Extract state tensors\n        device_states = {}\n        for i, (state_name, state_list) in enumerate(state_tensors.items(), start=2):\n            device_states[state_name] = cast(list[Optional[Tensor]], grouped_tensors_tuple[i])\n\n        # Check for sparse gradients in this device group\n        device_has_sparse_grad = has_sparse_grad and any(\n            grad.is_sparse for grad in device_grads\n        )\n\n        # Apply maximize\n        device_grads = _foreach_apply_maximize(device_grads, maximize)\n\n        #         &\\bf{return} \\:  \\theta_t                                                     \\\\[-1.ex]\n            &\\rule{110mm}{0.4pt}                                                          \\\\[-1.ex]\n       \\end{aligned}\n\n    For further details regarding the algorithm we refer to `Adam: A Method for Stochastic Optimization`_.\n    \"\"\"\n    + rf\"\"\"\n    Args:\n        {_params_doc}\n        lr (float, Tensor, optional): learning rate (default: 1e-3). A tensor LR\n            is not yet supported for all our implementations. Please use a float\n            LR if you are not also specifying fused=True or capturable=True.\n        betas (Tuple[float, float], optional): coefficients used for computing\n            running averages of gradient and its square (default: (0.9, 0.999))\n        eps (float, optional): term added to the denominator to improve\n            numerical stability (default: 1e-8)\n        weight_decay (float, optional): weight decay (L2 penalty) (default: 0)\n        decoupled_weight_decay (bool, optional): if True, this optimizer is\n            equivalent to AdamW and the algorithm will not accumulate weight\n            decay in the momentum nor variance. (default: False)\n        amsgrad (bool, optional): whether to use the AMSGrad variant of this\n            algorithm from the paper `On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond`_\n            (default: False)\n        {_foreach_doc}\n        {_maximize_doc}\n        {_capturable_doc}\n        {_differentiable_doc}\n        {_fused_doc}\n    .. Note::\n        A prototype implementation of Adam and AdamW for MPS supports `torch.float32` and `torch.float16`.\n    .. _Adam\\: A Method for Stochastic Optimization:\n        https://arxiv.org/abs/1412.6980\n    .. _On the Convergence of Adam and Beyond:\n        https://openreview.net/forum?id=ryQu7f-RZ\n\n    \"\"\"\n)\n\n\ndef _single_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    if torch.jit.is_scripting():\n        # this assert is due to JIT being dumb and not realizing that the ops below\n        # have overloads to handle both float and Tensor lrs, so we just assert it's\n        # a float since most people using JIT are using floats\n        assert isinstance(lr, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta1, float)\n        assert isinstance(beta2, float)\n    else:\n        lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n        # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    # Note: ensure type declaration is under conditional check for isinstance\n    # or else torchscript will get cranky about the DeviceDict type.\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDtypeDict] = {(beta1.device, beta1.dtype): beta1}\n    else:\n        beta1_dict = None\n\n    for i, param in enumerate(params):\n        grad = grads[i] if not maximize else -grads[i]\n        exp_avg = exp_avgs[i]\n        exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sqs[i]\n        step_t = state_steps[i]\n\n        # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n            capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices()\n            assert (\n                param.device.type == step_t.device.type\n                and param.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            ), (\n                f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n            )\n\n        # update step\n        step_t += 1\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                param.mul_(1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n                if differentiable and isinstance(weight_decay, Tensor):\n                    if weight_decay.requires_grad:\n                        grad = grad.addcmul_(param.clone(), weight_decay)\n                    else:\n                        grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    grad = grad.add(param, alpha=weight_decay)\n\n        if torch.is_complex(param):\n            grad = torch.view_as_real(grad)\n            exp_avg = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg)\n            exp_avg_sq = torch.view_as_real(exp_avg_sq)\n            if amsgrad:\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_real(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n            param = torch.view_as_real(param)\n\n        device = param.device\n\n        if beta1_dict is not None:\n            dtype = param.dtype  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n\n            # cast to workaround https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/140601\n            key = (device, dtype)\n            if key not in beta1_dict:\n                beta1_dict[key] = beta1.to(  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n                    device=device, dtype=dtype, non_blocking=True\n                )\n\n            device_beta1: Union[float, Tensor] = beta1_dict[key]\n        else:\n            device_beta1 = beta1\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        exp_avg.lerp_(grad, 1 - device_beta1)\n\n        # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n        if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n            if beta2.requires_grad:\n                # Using lerp to only use 2 operations bc addcmul's value cannot be a tensor\n                # Showing equivalence of differentiable path and nondifferentiable path\n                # expavg * b2 + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                #           add expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) = 0\n                # expavg * b2 + expavg * (1-b2) - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg - expavg * (1-b2) + grad^2 * (1-b2)\n                # expavg + (grad^2 - expavg) * (1-b2)\n                # expavg.lerp(grad^2, 1-beta2)\n                exp_avg_sq.lerp_(torch.square(grad), weight=1 - beta2)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(\n                    grad, grad, value=cast(float, 1 - beta2)\n                )\n        else:\n            exp_avg_sq.mul_(beta2).addcmul_(grad, grad, value=1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        if capturable or differentiable:\n            step = step_t\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n                if beta1.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n\n            # Nested if is necessary to bypass jitscript rules\n            if differentiable and isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n                if beta2.requires_grad:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2 ** step.clone()\n                else:\n                    bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n            else:\n                bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n            step_size_neg = step_size.neg()\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2.sqrt()\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                if differentiable:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i].clone()\n                else:\n                    max_exp_avg_sq = max_exp_avg_sqs[i]\n\n                max_exp_avg_sqs[i].copy_(torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sq, exp_avg_sq))\n\n                # Uses the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                # Folds in (admittedly ugly) 1-elem step_size math here to avoid extra param-set-sized read+write\n                # (can't fold it into addcdiv_ below because addcdiv_ requires value is a Number, not a Tensor)\n                denom = (\n                    max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n            else:\n                denom = (\n                    exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / (bias_correction2_sqrt * step_size_neg)\n                ).add_(eps / step_size_neg)\n\n            if differentiable:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg.clone(), denom)\n            else:\n                param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom)\n        else:\n            step = _get_value(step_t)\n\n            bias_correction1 = 1 - beta1**step\n            bias_correction2 = 1 - beta2**step\n\n            step_size = lr / bias_correction1\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2**0.5\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch.maximum(max_exp_avg_sqs[i], exp_avg_sq, out=max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                denom = (max_exp_avg_sqs[i].sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n            else:\n                denom = (exp_avg_sq.sqrt() / bias_correction2_sqrt).add_(eps)\n\n            param.addcdiv_(exp_avg, denom, value=-step_size)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n        # Lastly, switch back to complex view\n        if amsgrad and torch.is_complex(params[i]):\n            max_exp_avg_sqs[i] = torch.view_as_complex(max_exp_avg_sqs[i])\n\n\ndef _multi_tensor_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,\n    beta1: Union[float, Tensor],\n    beta2: Union[float, Tensor],\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n):\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    if isinstance(lr, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise RuntimeError(\n                \"lr as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if lr.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor lr must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta1, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta1 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta1.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta1 must be 1-element\")\n\n    if isinstance(beta2, Tensor):\n        if not capturable:\n            raise ValueError(\n                \"beta2 as a Tensor is not supported for capturable=False and foreach=True\"\n            )\n        if beta2.numel() != 1:\n            raise ValueError(\"Tensor beta2 must be 1-element\")\n\n    # If compiling, the compiler will handle cudagraph checks, see note [torch.compile x capturable]\n    if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and capturable:\n        capturable_supported_devices = _get_capturable_supported_devices(\n            supports_xla=False\n        )\n        assert all(\n            p.device.type == step.device.type\n            and p.device.type in capturable_supported_devices\n            for p, step in zip(params, state_steps)\n        ), (\n            f\"If capturable=True, params and state_steps must be on supported devices: {capturable_supported_devices}.\"\n        )\n\n    assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None\n\n    assert not differentiable, \"_foreach ops don't support autograd\"\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n    # TODO: Support nonzero-dim Tensor betas, see #147921\n\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the beta when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    beta1_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        {beta1.device: beta1}\n        if isinstance(beta1, Tensor) and str(beta1.device) != \"cpu\"\n        else None\n    )\n\n    for (\n        device_params_,\n        device_grads_,\n        device_exp_avgs_,\n        device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_max_exp_avg_sqs_,\n        device_state_steps_,\n    ), _ in grouped_tensors.values():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device = device_params[0].device\n        if beta1_dict is not None and device not in beta1_dict:\n            beta1_dict[device] = beta1.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr, attr-defined]\n\n        device_beta1 = beta1_dict[device] if beta1_dict else beta1\n\n        # Handle complex parameters\n        if has_complex:\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params,\n                    device_grads,\n                    device_exp_avgs,\n                    device_exp_avg_sqs,\n                    device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n                )\n            else:\n                _view_as_real(\n                    device_params, device_grads, device_exp_avgs, device_exp_avg_sqs\n                )\n\n        if maximize:\n            device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n        # Update steps\n        # If steps are on CPU, foreach will fall back to the slow path, which is a for-loop calling t.add(1) over\n        # and over. 1 will then be wrapped into a Tensor over and over again, which is slower than if we just\n        # wrapped it once now. The alpha is required to assure we go to the right overload.\n        if not torch.compiler.is_compiling() and device_state_steps[0].is_cpu:\n            torch._foreach_add_(\n                device_state_steps, torch.tensor(1.0, device=\"cpu\"), alpha=1.0\n            )\n        else:\n            torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n\n        if weight_decay != 0:\n            if decoupled_weight_decay:\n                # Perform stepweight decay\n                torch._foreach_mul_(device_params, 1 - lr * weight_decay)\n            else:\n                # Reuse the intermediate memory (device_grads) already allocated for maximize\n                if maximize:\n                    torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)\n                else:\n                    device_grads = torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[assignment]\n                        device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n                    )\n\n        # Decay the first and second moment running average coefficient\n        # Use device beta1 if beta1 is a tensor to ensure all\n        # tensors are on the same device\n        torch._foreach_lerp_(\n            device_exp_avgs, device_grads, cast(float, 1 - device_beta1)\n        )\n\n        torch._foreach_mul_(device_exp_avg_sqs, beta2)\n\n        # Due to the strictness of the _foreach_addcmul API, we can't have a single\n        # tensor scalar as the scalar arg (only python number is supported there)\n        # as a result, separate out the value mul\n        # Filed https://github.com/pytorch/pytorch/issues/139795\n        if isinstance(beta2, torch.Tensor):\n            scaled_device_grads = torch._foreach_mul(device_grads, 1 - beta2)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1.0\n        else:\n            scaled_device_grads = device_grads  # type: ignore[assignment]\n            value = 1 - beta2\n\n        torch._foreach_addcmul_(\n            device_exp_avg_sqs, scaled_device_grads, device_grads, value\n        )\n\n        # Delete the local intermediate(s) since they won't be used anymore to save on peak memory\n        del device_grads\n        del scaled_device_grads\n\n        bias_correction1: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n        bias_correction2_sqrt: Union[tuple[Tensor, ...], list[Tensor]]\n\n        if capturable:\n            bias_correction1 = torch._foreach_pow(beta1, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            bias_correction2 = torch._foreach_pow(beta2, device_state_steps)  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            # foreach_sub doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction1, 1)\n            torch._foreach_sub_(bias_correction2, 1)\n            # we do not negate bias_correction1 as it'll need to be negated later anyway\n            torch._foreach_neg_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # foreach_div doesn't allow a scalar as the first arg\n            torch._foreach_div_(bias_correction1, lr)\n            torch._foreach_reciprocal_(bias_correction1)\n\n            torch._foreach_sqrt_(bias_correction2)\n\n            # Re-assign for clarity as we maintain minimal intermediates: we'll have\n            # step_size = - lr / (1 - beta1 ^ t) where t = num_steps\n            # bias_correction2_sqrt = sqrt(1 - beta2 ^ t)\n            step_size = bias_correction1\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = bias_correction2\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)  # type: ignore[assignment]\n\n                # Set intermediate to the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient when amsgrad\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, step_size)\n\n            # at this point, exp_avg_sq_sqrt = - (1 - beta^t) * [sqrt(exp_avg_sq / (1 - beta2^t)) + eps] / lr\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(device_params, device_exp_avgs, exp_avg_sq_sqrt)\n        else:\n            bias_correction1 = [\n                1 - beta1 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n            ]\n            bias_correction2 = [\n                1 - beta2 ** _get_value(step) for step in device_state_steps\n            ]\n\n            step_size = _stack_if_compiling([(lr / bc) * -1 for bc in bias_correction1])\n\n            bias_correction2_sqrt = [bc**0.5 for bc in bias_correction2]  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n\n            if amsgrad:\n                device_max_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_max_exp_avg_sqs_)\n                # Maintains the maximum of all 2nd moment running avg. till now\n                torch._foreach_maximum_(device_max_exp_avg_sqs, device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n                # Use the max. for normalizing running avg. of gradient\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_max_exp_avg_sqs)\n            else:\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt = torch._foreach_sqrt(device_exp_avg_sqs)\n\n            torch._foreach_div_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, bias_correction2_sqrt)\n            torch._foreach_add_(exp_avg_sq_sqrt, eps)\n            torch._foreach_addcdiv_(\n                device_params,\n                device_exp_avgs,\n                exp_avg_sq_sqrt,\n                step_size,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            )\n\n\ndef _fused_adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor],\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor],\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    has_complex: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    capturable: bool,  # Needed for consistency.\n    differentiable: bool,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool,\n) -> None:\n    if not params:\n        return\n    if differentiable:\n        raise RuntimeError(\"Adam with fused=True does not support differentiable=True\")\n\n    grad_scale_dict: DeviceDict = (\n        {grad_scale.device: grad_scale} if grad_scale is not None else {}\n    )\n    found_inf_dict: DeviceDict = (\n        {found_inf.device: found_inf} if found_inf is not None else {}\n    )\n\n    # We only shuffle around the lr when it is a Tensor and on CUDA, otherwise, we prefer\n    # treating it as a scalar.\n    lr_dict: Optional[DeviceDict] = (\n        {lr.device: lr} if isinstance(lr, Tensor) and str(lr.device) != \"cpu\" else None\n    )\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        [params, grads, exp_avgs, exp_avg_sqs, max_exp_avg_sqs, state_steps]  # type: ignore[list-item]\n    )\n    for (device, _), (\n        (\n            device_params_,\n            device_grads_,\n            device_exp_avgs_,\n            device_exp_avg_sqs_,\n            device_max_exp_avg_sqs,\n            device_state_steps_,\n        ),\n        _,\n    ) in grouped_tensors.items():\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n        device_exp_avgs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avgs_)\n        device_exp_avg_sqs = cast(list[Tensor], device_exp_avg_sqs_)\n        device_state_steps = cast(list[Tensor], device_state_steps_)\n\n        device_grad_scale, device_found_inf = None, None\n        if grad_scale is not None:\n            device_grad_scale = grad_scale_dict.setdefault(\n                device, grad_scale.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n            )\n        if found_inf is not None:\n            device_found_inf = found_inf_dict.setdefault(\n                device, found_inf.to(device, non_blocking=True)\n            )\n        if lr_dict is not None and device not in lr_dict:\n            lr_dict[device] = lr.to(device=device, non_blocking=True)  # type: ignore[union-attr]\n            lr = lr_dict[device]\n        torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n        func = torch._fused_adam_ if not decoupled_weight_decay else torch._fused_adamw_\n        func(\n            device_params,\n            device_grads,\n            device_exp_avgs,\n            device_exp_avg_sqs,\n            device_max_exp_avg_sqs,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            device_state_steps,\n            amsgrad=amsgrad,\n            lr=lr,  # type: ignore[arg-type]\n            beta1=beta1,\n            beta2=beta2,\n            weight_decay=weight_decay,\n            eps=eps,\n            maximize=maximize,\n            grad_scale=device_grad_scale,\n            found_inf=device_found_inf,\n        )\n        if device_found_inf is not None:\n            torch._foreach_sub_(\n                device_state_steps, [device_found_inf] * len(device_state_steps)\n            )\n\n\n@_disable_dynamo_if_unsupported(single_tensor_fn=_single_tensor_adam)\ndef adam(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avgs: list[Tensor],\n    exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    max_exp_avg_sqs: list[Tensor],\n    state_steps: list[Tensor],\n    # kwonly args with defaults are not supported by functions compiled with torchscript issue #70627\n    # setting this as kwarg for now as functional API is compiled by torch/distributed/optim\n    foreach: Optional[bool] = None,\n    capturable: bool = False,\n    differentiable: bool = False,\n    fused: Optional[bool] = None,\n    grad_scale: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    found_inf: Optional[Tensor] = None,\n    has_complex: bool = False,\n    decoupled_weight_decay: bool = False,\n    *,\n    amsgrad: bool,\n    beta1: float,\n    beta2: float,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    eps: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n):\n    r\"\"\"Functional API that performs Adam algorithm computation.\n\n    See :class:`~torch.optim.Adam` for details.\n    \"\"\"\n    # type: ignore[index]\n            device_found_inf = found_inf_dict[device]  # type: ignore[index]\n        torch._foreach_add_(device_state_steps, 1)\n        torch._fused_adagrad_(\n            device_params,\n            device_grads,\n            device_state_sums,\n            device_state_steps,\n            lr=lr,\n            lr_decay=lr_decay,\n            weight_decay=weight_decay,\n            eps=eps,\n            maximize=maximize,\n            grad_scale=device_grad_scale,\n            found_inf=device_found_inf,\n        )\n        if device_found_inf is not None:\n            torch._foreach_sub_(\n                device_state_steps, [device_found_inf] * len(device_state_steps)\n            )\n",

  "plan": "# Task: Extract Shared Foreach Optimizer Step\n\n## Context\nThe PyTorch optimizer implementations contain repeated `_multi_tensor_*` patterns across 11+ optimizer files. These functions have common preprocessing patterns that can be extracted to reduce duplication.\n\n## Exploration Results\n\n### Common Patterns Found Across _multi_tensor_* Functions\n1. **Empty parameter check**: All return early if `len(params) == 0`\n2. **LR scalar conversion**: `lr = _to_scalar(lr)`\n3. **Tensor grouping**: `Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype([...], with_indices=True)`\n4. **Maximize handling**: `if maximize: device_grads = torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)`\n5. **Weight decay**: Memory-optimized addition with reuse of intermediate tensors\n6. **Assertions**: `assert not differentiable` and `assert grad_scale is None and found_inf is None`\n7. **Complex dtype handling**: `_view_as_real(...)` pattern\n8. **CPU step optimization**: Avoid repeated tensor wrapping for CPU-resident state\n\n### Utilities Available for Reuse\nFrom `torch.optim.optimizer`:\n- `_to_scalar()` - Convert tensor LR to scalar\n- `_get_value()` - Extract Python value from tensor\n- `_view_as_real()` - Convert complex tensors for processing\n- `_get_scalar_dtype()`, `_get_capturable_supported_devices()`\n- Type aliases: `DeviceDict`, `DeviceDtypeDict`\n- `Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype()` - Core grouping utility\n\n### Optimizer-Specific Differences\n- **SGD**: Momentum buffer handling, sparse gradient fallback\n- **Adam**: Parameter validation, step increment, decoupled weight decay, AMSGrad logic\n- **RMSprop**: Complex handling, centered variance, CPU step optimization\n- **Adagrad**: Sparse gradient fallback, LR decay per parameter\n- Each has distinct bias correction and state update logic that can't be fully abstracted\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Approach: Helper Functions + Callback-based Framework\n\nCreate `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` with:\n\n1. **Helper functions for common operations**:\n   - `_foreach_apply_maximize(device_grads, maximize)` - Negate gradients if maximizing\n   - `_foreach_apply_weight_decay(device_grads, device_params, weight_decay, maximize)` - Memory-optimized weight decay\n   - `_foreach_group_tensors_and_prepare(params, grads, state_tensors, maximize, weight_decay, **kwargs)` - Groups and preprocesses tensors\n\n2. **Main callback-based orchestration function**:\n   - `_foreach_optimizer_step(params, grads, step_fn, state_tensors, **kwargs)`\n   - Handles grouping, assertions, maximize, weight decay\n   - Calls `step_fn(device_params, device_grads, device_states, indices, **kwargs)` for optimizer-specific logic\n\n3. **Common utility functions**:\n   - `_get_group_device_dtype()` - Extract device/dtype from grouped tensors\n   - `_validate_foreach_hyperparams()` - Common validation for tensor hyperparameters\n\n### Files to Modify\n\n**Primary**:\n- Create: `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` with shared logic\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/sgd.py` - Use _foreach_optimizer_step\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adam.py` - Use _foreach_optimizer_step\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adamw.py` - Inherits from Adam (automatic)\n\n**Secondary** (to meet \u22653 file requirement + reduce duplication):\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adagrad.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/rmsprop.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/radam.py` - Use shared helpers\n- Update: `/workspace/torch/optim/adadelta.py` - Use shared helpers\n\n## Detailed Implementation Plan\n\n### Step 1: Create `torch/optim/_foreach.py`\n\n```python\n# torch/optim/_foreach.py\nfrom typing import Callable, cast, Optional, Union, Any\nimport torch\nfrom torch import Tensor\nfrom .optimizer import (\n    _to_scalar, _get_value, _view_as_real,\n    Optimizer, DeviceDict, DeviceDtypeDict\n)\n\n# Helper functions\ndef _foreach_apply_maximize(\n    device_grads: list[Tensor],\n    maximize: bool\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"Apply maximize (negate grads) and return modified grads.\"\"\"\n    if maximize:\n        return torch._foreach_neg(device_grads)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n    return device_grads\n\ndef _foreach_apply_weight_decay(\n    device_grads: list[Tensor],\n    device_params: list[Tensor],\n    weight_decay: float,\n    maximize: bool,\n    can_reuse_grads: bool = True\n) -> list[Tensor]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Apply weight decay to gradients with memory optimization.\n\n    When maximize has already allocated new memory for device_grads,\n    we can reuse that memory. Otherwise, allocate new memory.\n    \"\"\"\n    if weight_decay == 0:\n        return device_grads\n\n    # Reuse device_grads memory if it was already allocated for maximize\n    if can_reuse_grads and maximize:\n        torch._foreach_add_(device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n        return device_grads\n    else:\n        return torch._foreach_add(  # type: ignore[attr-defined]\n            device_grads, device_params, alpha=weight_decay\n        )\n\ndef _foreach_optimizer_step(\n    params: list[Tensor],\n    grads: list[Tensor],\n    step_fn: Callable[..., None],\n    state_tensors: dict[str, list[Optional[Tensor]]],\n    has_sparse_grad: bool = False,\n    maximize: bool = False,\n    weight_decay: float = 0.0,\n    lr: Union[float, Tensor] = 1e-3,\n    **kwargs: Any\n) -> None:\n    \"\"\"\n    Shared foreach optimizer step with common preprocessing.\n\n    Args:\n        params: List of parameters to optimize\n        grads: List of gradients\n        step_fn: Callback function that implements optimizer-specific logic\n        state_tensors: Dict mapping state names to lists of state tensors\n        has_sparse_grad: Whether sparse gradients are possible\n        maximize: Whether to maximize loss instead of minimize\n        weight_decay: Weight decay factor\n        lr: Learning rate\n        **kwargs: Additional arguments passed to step_fn\n    \"\"\"\n    if len(params) == 0:\n        return\n\n    lr = _to_scalar(lr)\n\n    # Group all tensors by device and dtype\n    tensors_to_group = [params, grads] + list(state_tensors.values())\n    grouped_tensors = Optimizer._group_tensors_by_device_and_dtype(\n        tensors_to_group,\n        with_indices=True,\n    )\n\n    for grouped_tensors_tuple, indices in grouped_tensors.values():\n        # Extract grouped tensors\n        device_params_ = grouped_tensors_tuple[0]\n        device_grads_ = grouped_tensors_tuple[1]\n        device_params = cast(list[Tensor], device_params_)\n        device_grads = cast(list[Tensor], device_grads_)\n\n        # Extract state tensors\n        device_states = {}\n        for i, (state_name, state_list) in enumerate(state_tensors.items(), start=2):\n            device_states[state_name] = cast(list[Optional[Tensor]], grouped_tensors_tuple[i])\n\n        # Check for sparse gradients in this device group\n        device_has_sparse_grad = has_sparse_grad and any(\n            grad.is_sparse for grad in device_grads\n        )\n\n        # Apply maximize\n        device_grads = _foreach_apply_maximize(device_grads, maximize)\n\n        # Apply weight decay\n        device_grads = _foreach_apply_weight_decay(\n            device_grads, device_params, weight_decay, maximize\n        )\n\n        # Call optimizer-specific step function\n        step_fn(\n            device_params=device_params,\n            device_grads=device_grads,\n            device_states=device_states,\n            device_has_sparse_grad=device_has_sparse_grad,\n            indices=indices,\n            lr=lr,\n            **kwargs\n        )\n```\n\n### Step 2: Refactor SGD's `_multi_tensor_sgd`\n\nReplace the common preprocessing with `_foreach_optimizer_step` while keeping momentum-specific logic.\n\n### Step 3: Refactor Adam's `_multi_tensor_adam`\n\nApply same pattern, keeping Adam-specific logic (step increment, bias correction, AMSGrad).\n\n### Step 4: Update Other Optimizers\n\nIncrementally refactor Adagrad, RMSprop, RAdam to use shared helpers.\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n1. **Callback approach**: Keep optimizer-specific logic in a step_fn callback to avoid forcing all optimizers into the same mold\n2. **Memory efficiency**: Maintain the existing memory-reuse optimization (e.g., reusing device_grads when maximize is applied)\n3. **Gradual refactoring**: Don't require all optimizers to change at once; allow phased migration\n4. **Backward compatibility**: Existing public APIs unchanged; only internal _multi_tensor_* functions refactored\n5. **Type safety**: Use cast() appropriately and preserve existing type hints\n\n## Testing Strategy\n\n1. Run existing optimizer tests: `python -m pytest test/test_optim.py -xvs`\n2. Verify numerical equivalence between old and new implementations\n3. Check that state_dict serialization still works\n4. Ensure hook APIs still fire in correct order\n5. Validate LR scheduler integration\n\n## Success Criteria Verification\n\n- [ ] `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` created with shared logic\n- [ ] At least 3 optimizer files import from _foreach (SGD, Adam, Adagrad)\n- [ ] Duplicate foreach patterns reduced (code duplications removed)\n- [ ] Original optimizer APIs still work (all tests pass)\n- [ ] No performance regressions\n\n## Critical Files\n\n### To Create:\n- `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py`\n\n### To Modify:\n- `/workspace/torch/optim/sgd.py` (lines 378-471 of _multi_tensor_sgd)\n- `/workspace/torch/optim/adam.py` (lines 544-787 of _multi_tensor_adam)\n- `/workspace/torch/optim/adagrad.py` (lines ~388-495 of _multi_tensor_adagrad)\n\n### Utilities to Import:\nFrom `torch.optim.optimizer`:\n- `_to_scalar`, `_get_value`, `_view_as_real`\n- `Optimizer`, `DeviceDict`, `DeviceDtypeDict`\n\n## Implementation Notes\n\n1. The _foreach_optimizer_step function signature is flexible to accept any state tensors\n2. Each optimizer's step_fn is responsible for its own logic (momentum, exponential moving averages, etc.)\n3. The shared function handles the \"mechanical\" parts: grouping, maximize, weight_decay\n4. Complex dtype handling will need special treatment - may need helper or documented pattern\n5. Sparse gradient handling varies by optimizer - kept in step_fn for now\n\n## Status: READY FOR IMPLEMENTATION\nPlan is complete and ready for execution. User approval requested.\n"

Core grouping utility\n\n### Optimizer-Specific Differences\n- **SGD**: Momentum buffer handling, sparse gradient fallback\n- **Adam**: Parameter validation, step increment, decoupled weight decay, AMSGrad logic\n- **RMSprop**: Complex handling, centered variance, CPU step optimization\n- **Adagrad**: Sparse gradient fallback, LR decay per parameter\n- Each has distinct bias correction and state update logic that can't be fully abstracted\n\n## Implementation Strategy\n\n### Approach: Helper Functions + Callback-based Framework\n\nCreate `/workspace/torch/optim/_foreach.py` with:\n\n1. **Helper functions for common operations**:\n   -
